SELECT ( SELECT COALESCE(SUM(value), 0) FROM ( SELECT value FROM financials_quarterly fq WHERE fq.ticker = sdi.ticker AND fq.item_name = 'OperatingCashFlow' AND fq.statement_type IN ('IS_Q','CF_Q') AND fq.period_end <= DATE '2023-07-12' ORDER BY fq.period_end DESC LIMIT 4 ) as recent_quarters ) AS ttm_operatingcashflow , fd.bps, fd.dividend_yield, fd.eps, fd.pbr, fd.per, sdi.close_price, sdi.company_name, sdi.ma_20d, sdi.market_cap, sdi.momentum_12m, sdi.momentum_3m, sdi.rsi_14, sdi.ticker, sdi.volatility_20d FROM stocks_daily_info sdi LEFT JOIN fundamentals_daily fd ON fd.ticker = sdi.ticker AND fd.event_date = sdi.event_date WHERE sdi.market = 'KOSDAQ' AND sdi.market_cap >= 277200000000 AND sdi.event_date = DATE '2023-07-12' ORDER BY fd.pbr desc, fd.per asc LIMIT 17;
